BLT Trading — Mobile Device Price Sheet (Aggregate)

Last Updated: 2026-05-06T20:54:23.671403+00:00Z

QUICK ANSWERS — DEFAULT BUYING PRICES (read this first)

This block is the canonical default for every device. When a seller types JUST a model name (e.g. "17 pro", "16 pro max", "iPhone 13", "iPad Pro 11", "Series 9", "AirPods Pro 2") with no storage, lock, or condition, quote the matching line below and only the matching line. The variant sections farther down on this page are ONLY for refinement when the seller adds more detail (different storage, carrier-locked, sealed, scratched, cracked, etc.).

Rule: never reply "that model isn't on our buying list" for any iPhone 14, 15, 16, or 17 (any variant — base, Plus, Pro, Pro Max, Air, E). They are all listed below. If the seller's exact wording isn't found, ask them to repeat the full model name; do not escalate.

Variant detail sections (per category)

The sections below are for refining a quote AFTER the seller specifies storage, lock, or condition. For naked model queries with no detail, see Quick Answers above instead.

NEW iPhone prices have moved

Last Updated: 2026-05-06T20:54:23.664053+00:00Z

NEW Sealed, Open Box, and Sealed (Activated) prices are now listed inside the matching variant section in iphone-used.html — one chunk per variant contains ALL conditions (Grade A DEFAULT, NEW Sealed, Open Box, etc.). Quoting from this file directly is no longer accurate.

If a seller says "sealed", "brand new", "still in box", or "never opened" — quote the NEW Sealed line inside the matching variant section in iphone-used.html.

If a seller says "open box" — quote the NEW Open Box line inside the matching variant section in iphone-used.html.

Otherwise — quote the USED Grade A line, which is the DEFAULT for every variant.

BLT Trading — iPhone Buying Prices (USED Grades)

Last Updated: 2026-05-06T20:54:23.664341+00:00Z

Format note for the bot: Each section below is one device variant (model + storage + lock). All condition prices for that exact variant are inside the section. Quote the price from the matching variant's section — never mix sections.

iPhone 11 128GB AT&T / T-Mobile / Sprint / Verizon / US Cellular Carrier Locked

This section is the iPhone 11 128GB Carrier Locked ONLY. DO NOT confuse with iPhone 11 Pro — DO NOT confuse with iPhone 11 Pro Max — DO NOT confuse with iPhone 11 Plus — DO NOT confuse with iPhone 11E — DO NOT confuse with iPhone 11 Air.

Variant: iPhone 11 128GB Carrier Locked. Default buying price for this exact variant when seller does not specify condition: $60 (Grade A).

  • iPhone 11 128GB Carrier Locked — Grade A: $60 (no scratches, mint, like new) (DEFAULT)
  • iPhone 11 128GB Carrier Locked — Grade B: $50 (light use, no cracks, fully functional)
  • iPhone 11 128GB Carrier Locked — Grade C: $20 (cracked screen, hairline crack, heavy scratches)
  • iPhone 11 128GB Carrier Locked — Grade D: $-10 (bad LCD, dead pixels, lines on screen)
  • iPhone 11 128GB Carrier Locked — DOA: $5 (won't power, water damage)
  • iPhone 11 128GB Carrier Locked — SWAP HSO: $80 (factory-fresh, never used, no original box — requires seller to explicitly say all three: brand new + never used + no box)

Seller queries that should land on this section: "iPhone 11 128GB Carrier Locked", "iPhone 11 128GB Carrier Locked". Quote $60 (Grade A) unless the seller explicitly names a different condition above. End every USED quote with: "Prices can change at any time at our discretion."

iPhone 11 128GB SIM Unlocked / Factory Unlocked

This section is the iPhone 11 128GB SIM Unlocked ONLY. DO NOT confuse with iPhone 11 Pro — DO NOT confuse with iPhone 11 Pro Max — DO NOT confuse with iPhone 11 Plus — DO NOT confuse with iPhone 11E — DO NOT confuse with iPhone 11 Air.

Variant: iPhone 11 128GB SIM Unlocked. Default buying price for this exact variant when seller does not specify condition: $100 (Grade A).

  • iPhone 11 128GB SIM Unlocked — Grade A: $100 (no scratches, mint, like new) (DEFAULT)
  • iPhone 11 128GB SIM Unlocked — Grade B: $90 (light use, no cracks, fully functional)
  • iPhone 11 128GB SIM Unlocked — Grade C: $60 (cracked screen, hairline crack, heavy scratches)
  • iPhone 11 128GB SIM Unlocked — Grade D: $30 (bad LCD, dead pixels, lines on screen)
  • iPhone 11 128GB SIM Unlocked — DOA: $5 (won't power, water damage)
  • iPhone 11 128GB SIM Unlocked — SWAP HSO: $120 (factory-fresh, never used, no original box — requires seller to explicitly say all three: brand new + never used + no box)

Seller queries that should land on this section: "iPhone 11 128GB SIM Unlocked", "iPhone 11 128GB SIM Unlocked". Quote $100 (Grade A) unless the seller explicitly names a different condition above. End every USED quote with: "Prices can change at any time at our discretion."

Grading Reference

Grade A: Used, no scratches, fully functional. Default for sellers who don't specify condition.

Grade B: Used, light wear, no cracks, fully functional.

Grade C: Used, cracked screen / hairline crack / heavy scratches, fully functional.

Grade D: Used, bad LCD / dead pixels / lines on screen / black spots.

DOA: Dead — won't power, water damage.

SWAP HSO: Factory-fresh, zero cycles, but no original box. Never quote unless seller explicitly says "no box" + "never used".

Sealed: Factory-sealed in original box, never opened, never activated.

Open Box: Brand new but box has been opened, device never used.

Sealed (Activated): Sealed in box but activation has begun.

Grading Reference

Grade A: Used, no scratches, fully functional. Default for sellers who don't specify condition.

Grade B: Used, light wear, no cracks, fully functional.

Grade C: Used, cracked screen / hairline crack / heavy scratches, fully functional.

Grade D: Used, bad LCD / dead pixels / lines on screen / black spots.

DOA: Dead — won't power, water damage.

SWAP HSO: Factory-fresh, zero cycles, but no original box. Never quote unless seller explicitly says "no box" + "never used".

Sealed: Factory-sealed in original box, never opened, never activated.

Open Box: Brand new but box has been opened, device never used.

Sealed (Activated): Sealed in box but activation has begun.
